<p><b>Safaree Lloyd Samuels</b> (born July 4, 1981)<sup id=3D"cite_ref-2" c=
lass=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Safaree_Samuels=
#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup> is an American rapper. He started his musical c=
areer in the group the Hoodstars in the early 2000s alongside rapper <a hre=
f=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nicki_Minaj" title=3D"Nicki Minaj">Nicki=
 Minaj</a>. Samuels is also known as a solo artist. In 2016, he joined the =
cast of the <a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/VH1" title=3D"VH1">VH1=
</a> reality show <i><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Love_%26_Hip_=
Hop:_Hollywood" title=3D"Love &amp; Hip Hop: Hollywood">Love &amp; Hip Hop:=
 Hollywood</a></i>. In 2017, he moved back to his hometown of <a href=3D"ht=
tps://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_York_City" title=3D"New York City">New York=
 City</a> and joined the cast of <i><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wik=
i/Love_%26_Hip_Hop:_New_York" title=3D"Love &amp; Hip Hop: New York">Love &=
amp; Hip Hop: New York</a></i>.
</p>
<meta property=3D"mw:PageProp/toc">
<h2><span class=3D"mw-headline" id=3D"Early_life_and_education">Early life =
and education</span><span class=3D"mw-editsection"><span class=3D"mw-editse=
ction-bracket">[</span><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?titl=
e=3DSafaree_Samuels&amp;action=3Dedit&amp;section=3D1&amp;editintro=3DTempl=
ate:BLP_editintro" title=3D"Edit section: Early life and education">edit</a=
><span class=3D"mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Safaree Lloyd Samuels was born in the <a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.or=
g/wiki/Brooklyn" title=3D"Brooklyn">Brooklyn</a> borough of <a href=3D"http=
s://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_York_City" title=3D"New York City">New York C=
ity</a> on July 4, 1981, to immigrant <a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/w=
iki/Afro-Jamaicans" title=3D"Afro-Jamaicans">Jamaican</a> parents. He has t=
wo sisters, Shaneequa and Samantha.<sup id=3D"cite_ref-3" class=3D"referenc=
e"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Safaree_Samuels#cite_note-3">[3=
]</a></sup><sup id=3D"cite_ref-4" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en=
.wikipedia.org/wiki/Safaree_Samuels#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup> He attended =
<a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Midwood_High_School" title=3D"Midw=
ood High School">Midwood High School</a>.<sup id=3D"cite_ref-5" class=3D"re=
ference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Safaree_Samuels#cite_note=
-5">[5]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class=3D"mw-headline" id=3D"Career">Career</span><span class=3D"m=
w-editsection"><span class=3D"mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href=3D"ht=
tps://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=3DSafaree_Samuels&amp;action=3Dedi=
t&amp;section=3D2&amp;editintro=3DTemplate:BLP_editintro" title=3D"Edit sec=
tion: Career">edit</a><span class=3D"mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span=
></h2>
<p>Samuels started his musical career in the group the Hoodstars, formed in=
 the early 2000s with rappers <a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nick=
i_Minaj" title=3D"Nicki Minaj">Nicki Minaj</a>, Loustar, and Seven Up.<sup =
id=3D"cite_ref-6" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/w=
iki/Safaree_Samuels#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup> In 2004, the group recorded =
the entrance song for <a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Women_in_WWE=
" title=3D"Women in WWE">WWE Diva</a> <a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/w=
iki/Lisa_Marie_Varon" title=3D"Lisa Marie Varon">Victoria</a>, "Don't Mess =
With", which was featured on the compilation album <i><a href=3D"https://en=
.wikipedia.org/wiki/ThemeAddict:_WWE_The_Music,_Vol._6" title=3D"ThemeAddic=
t: WWE The Music, Vol. 6">ThemeAddict: WWE The Music, Vol. 6</a></i>.<sup i=
d=3D"cite_ref-7" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wi=
ki/Safaree_Samuels#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup> After the group disbanded, Mi=
naj started her solo career and Samuels supported her as a <a href=3D"https=
://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hype_man" title=3D"Hype man">hype man</a>.<sup id=
=3D"cite_ref-8" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wik=
i/Safaree_Samuels#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2012, he appeared in Minaj's music video "<a href=3D"https://en.w=
ikipedia.org/wiki/Stupid_Hoe" title=3D"Stupid Hoe">Stupid Hoe</a>".<sup id=
=3D"cite_ref-9" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wik=
i/Safaree_Samuels#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup> In 2012, Minaj released her se=
cond album, <i><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Pink_Friday:_Roman_=
Reloaded" title=3D"Pink Friday: Roman Reloaded">Pink Friday: Roman Reloaded=
</a></i>, where Samuels has six writing credits and was featured on the tra=
ck "Press Conference".<sup id=3D"cite_ref-10" class=3D"reference"><a href=
=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Safaree_Samuels#cite_note-10">[10]</a></s=
up>
</p><p>In 2015, Samuels released the mixtapes, <i>It Is What It Is</i> and =
<i>It Is What It Is, Vol. 2</i>.<sup id=3D"cite_ref-Mixtape1_11-0" class=3D=
"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Safaree_Samuels#cite_n=
ote-Mixtape1-11">[11]</a></sup><sup id=3D"cite_ref-Mixtape2_12-0" class=3D"=
reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Safaree_Samuels#cite_no=
te-Mixtape2-12">[12]</a></sup> In early 2016, he made appearance in the sec=
ond season of <i><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/K._Michelle:_My_L=
ife" title=3D"K. Michelle: My Life">K. Michelle: My Life</a></i>.<sup id=3D=
"cite_ref-13" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/=
Safaree_Samuels#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup> In May 2016, it was announced =
that Samuels joined the cast of the <a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wik=
i/VH1" title=3D"VH1">VH1</a> reality show <i><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedi=
a.org/wiki/Love_%26_Hip_Hop:_Hollywood" title=3D"Love &amp; Hip Hop: Hollyw=
ood">Love &amp; Hip Hop: Hollywood</a></i> for its third season, which prem=
iered in August 2016.<sup id=3D"cite_ref-14" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D=
"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Safaree_Samuels#cite_note-14">[14]</a></sup>=
<sup id=3D"cite_ref-15" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia=
.org/wiki/Safaree_Samuels#cite_note-15">[15]</a></sup> In July 2016, he rel=
eased a new mixtape titled <i>Real Yard Vibes</i>.<sup id=3D"cite_ref-RYV_1=
6-0" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Safaree_S=
amuels#cite_note-RYV-16">[16]</a></sup> In August 2017, it was announced th=
at Samuels would compete in the first season of VH1's <i><a href=3D"https:/=
/en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scared_Famous_(TV_series)" title=3D"Scared Famous (T=
V series)">Scared Famous</a></i>, which premiered in October 2017.<sup id=
=3D"cite_ref-17" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wi=
ki/Safaree_Samuels#cite_note-17">[17]</a></sup>
</p><p>In February 2018, Samuels was honored with a Blue &amp; Bougie Impac=
t Award.<sup id=3D"cite_ref-18" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.w=
ikipedia.org/wiki/Safaree_Samuels#cite_note-18">[18]</a></sup> In the same =
month, a nude picture and video of Samuels was leaked online.<sup id=3D"cit=
e_ref-19" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Safa=
ree_Samuels#cite_note-19">[19]</a></sup> In 2019, Samuels debuted the "Anac=
onda" line of <a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dildo" title=3D"Dild=
o">dildos</a> molded from his own penis.<sup id=3D"cite_ref-20" class=3D"re=
ference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Safaree_Samuels#cite_note=
-20">[20]</a></sup> In 2020, Samuels launched an <a href=3D"https://en.wiki=
pedia.org/wiki/OnlyFans" title=3D"OnlyFans">OnlyFans</a> account sharing hi=
s <a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Amateur_pornography" title=3D"Am=
ateur pornography">amateur pornographic</a> videos for $20 per month.<sup i=
d=3D"cite_ref-21" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/w=
iki/Safaree_Samuels#cite_note-21">[21]</a></sup><sup id=3D"cite_ref-22" cla=
ss=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Safaree_Samuels#c=
ite_note-22">[22]</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class=3D"mw-headline" id=3D"Personal_life">Personal life</span><s=
pan class=3D"mw-editsection"><span class=3D"mw-editsection-bracket">[</span=
><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=3DSafaree_Samuels&am=
p;action=3Dedit&amp;section=3D3&amp;editintro=3DTemplate:BLP_editintro" tit=
le=3D"Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class=3D"mw-editsection-br=
acket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Samuels dated rapper <a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nicki_Mina=
j" title=3D"Nicki Minaj">Nicki Minaj</a> from 2000<sup class=3D"noprint Inl=
ine-Template Template-Fact" style=3D"white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href=3D"ht=
tps://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title=3D"Wikipedia:C=
itation needed"><span title=3D"This claim needs references to reliable sour=
ces. (October 2021)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup> until their brea=
kup in 2014.<sup id=3D"cite_ref-23" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://=
en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Safaree_Samuels#cite_note-23">[23]</a></sup> Several =
tracks on Minaj's third album <i><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/T=
he_Pinkprint" title=3D"The Pinkprint">The Pinkprint</a></i> are believed to=
 have been inspired by the end of their relationship.<sup id=3D"cite_ref-24=
" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Safaree_Samu=
els#cite_note-24">[24]</a></sup> In 2016, he attempted to sue Minaj and acc=
used her of not crediting him on <i>The Pinkprint</i>.<sup id=3D"cite_ref-2=
5" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Safaree_Sam=
uels#cite_note-25">[25]</a></sup>
</p><p>He became engaged to actress <a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wik=
i/Erica_Mena" title=3D"Erica Mena">Erica Mena</a> on <a href=3D"https://en.=
wikipedia.org/wiki/Christmas_Eve" title=3D"Christmas Eve">Christmas Eve</a>=
 2018.<sup id=3D"cite_ref-26" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wik=
ipedia.org/wiki/Safaree_Samuels#cite_note-26">[26]</a></sup><sup id=3D"cite=
_ref-27" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Safar=
ee_Samuels#cite_note-27">[27]</a></sup> The couple married on October 7, 20=
19.<sup id=3D"cite_ref-28" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipe=
dia.org/wiki/Safaree_Samuels#cite_note-28">[28]</a></sup> On February 3, 20=
20, Samuels and Mena welcomed their daughter.<sup id=3D"cite_ref-29" class=
=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Safaree_Samuels#cit=
e_note-29">[29]</a></sup> On May 4, 2021, he announced that he and Mena wer=
e expecting their second child together.<sup id=3D"cite_ref-30" class=3D"re=
ference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Safaree_Samuels#cite_note=
-30">[30]</a></sup> On May 25, 2021, <a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wi=
ki/TMZ" title=3D"TMZ">TMZ</a> reported that Mena officially filed for divor=
ce from Samuels.<sup id=3D"cite_ref-31" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"http=
s://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Safaree_Samuels#cite_note-31">[31]</a></sup> On J=
une 28, 2021, he announced the arrival of their second child, a boy.<sup id=
=3D"cite_ref-32" class=3D"reference"><a href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wi=
ki/Safaree_Samuels#cite_note-32">[32]</a></sup> He's currently dating <i><a=
 href=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Love_%26_Hip_Hop:_Miami" title=3D"Lo=
ve &amp; Hip Hop: Miami">Love &amp; Hip Hop: Miami</a></i> co-star <a href=
=3D"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Amara_La_Negra" title=3D"Amara La Negra">=
Amara La Negra</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class=3D"mw-headline" id=3D"Discography">Discography</span><span =
class=3D"mw-editsection"><span class=3D"mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a =

<h3><span class=3D"mw-headline" id=3D"Mixtapes">Mixtapes</span><span class=

n></span></h3>

<tr>
